### [1] [Orbital evolution of asymmetric binaries within accreting environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18341)
*Albert Radulea,Marcelo E. Rubio,Konstantinos Kritos,Andrea Maselli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了吸积盘中极端质量比旋进体的长期演化，发现盘诱导耗散驱动轨道先快速与盘面对齐，再缓慢阻尼偏心率；相对论效应即使在远距离也会累积偏差，且吸积盘模型的选择对演化速率有显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解极端质量比旋进体嵌入吸积盘时，相对论轨道动力学与环境效应（盘相互作用）之间的耦合机制，以及这种耦合对长期演化的影响。

Method: 基于Kerr测地线建模轨道运动，通过有效质量吸积和动力学摩擦描述盘相互作用，构建框架研究致密天体反复穿越吸积盘时的长期演化，并对比Sirko-Goodman与Novikov-Thorne两种盘模型。

Result: 盘诱导耗散驱动两阶段演化：轨道面快速与盘面对齐，随后偏心率缓慢阻尼。相对论效应在远距离也会累积偏差，且偏差随轨道相对论性增强而加剧。相对论盘结构（更低密度、更大标高）导致更弱的轨道耗散和更慢的长期演化。中心黑洞自旋对整体圆化效率影响较小。

Conclusion: 研究一致建模相对论轨道动力学和吸积盘结构对于研究AGN盘中致密天体长期演化至关重要，为解释准周期爆发等现象提供框架。

Abstract: Extreme mass-ratio inspirals embedded in accretion disks provide a natural arena for studying the interplay between relativistic orbital dynamics and environmental effects. In this work, we develop a framework to investigate the secular evolution of compact objects repeatedly crossing an accretion disk around a supermassive black hole. The orbital motion is modeled through Kerr geodesics, while disk interactions are encoded through effective prescriptions for mass accretion and dynamical friction. We find that disk-induced dissipation generically drives a two-stage evolution characterized by rapid alignment of the orbital plane with the disk, followed by slower eccentricity damping. By systematically comparing the dynamics with a purely Keplerian treatment, we show that cumulative relativistic effects produce deviations even at large orbital separations, where the Keplerian approximation would naively be expected to remain accurate. These discrepancies grow through repeated disk crossings and become increasingly pronounced in more relativistic orbital configurations. We further investigate the impact of the accretion-disk model by comparing the Sirko-Goodman and Novikov-Thorne prescriptions. Relativistic disk structures predict systematically lower densities and larger scale heights, leading to weaker orbital dissipation and slower secular evolution. By contrast, the spin of the central black hole has only a minor effect on the overall circularization efficiency. Our results demonstrate the importance of consistently modeling both relativistic orbital dynamics and disk structure when studying compact objects embedded in AGN disks, and provide a framework for exploring their long-term evolution, as well as a possible connection to quasi-periodic eruptions.

</details>


### [2] [A matrix free action of the Ashtekar-Lewandowski volume operator of loop quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18397)
*Waleed Sherif*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无矩阵化的AL体积算符作用方法，利用Brunnemann-Thiemann密度表达式与Balakrishnan-Stieltjes表示，通过平移-预解求积(SRQ)近似体积算符，避免了稠密矩阵分解，实现了高自旋截断下的数值计算与谱分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 圈量子引力中AL体积算符的顶点作用通常依赖有限重耦矩阵的稠密谱分解，这阻碍了在大运动学Hilbert空间或高价顶点上的数值分析，亟需一种可扩展的无矩阵方法。

Method: 利用Brunnemann-Thiemann定向体积密度Q_v的矩阵元局部生成方式，基于Balakrishnan-Stieltjes表示将体积近似为(Q_v^2)^{1/4}，通过平移-预解求积(SRQ)实现作用——仅需重复应用Q_v和平移正定线性求解，兼容多移位Krylov方法。

Result: 严格证明了体积核的精确保持，给出了算子范数和残差误差估计，讨论了扇区缩放界；在嵌入K5图上验证了方法，数值模拟显示顶点期望值快速收敛、零体积模式精确保持；实现了自旋截断2j=250000下的无矩阵蒙特卡洛估计，并结合随机Lanczos求积估计了固定扇区的体积谱测度。

Conclusion: SRQ方法有效克服了稠密矩阵分解的瓶颈，为高自旋、高价顶点下体积算符的数值分析提供了一种可扩展且精确的方案。

Abstract: The Ashtekar-Lewandowski (AL) volume operator of loop quantum gravity is central to the Hamiltonian constraint, but its vertex action is usually obtained from dense spectral decompositions of finite recoupling matrices, obstructing numerical analysis on large kinematical Hilbert spaces or high-valence vertices. We formulate a matrix free action of the $SU(2)$ AL vertex volume operator in standard recoupling basis, making use of the Brunnemann-Thiemann expression for the oriented AL volume density $Q_{v}$ whose matrix elements can be generated locally from recoupling theory without forming the full matrix. Based on the Balakrishnan-Stieltjes representation of $(Q_{v}^{2})^{1/4}$ we approximate the volume by shifted-resolvent quadrature (SRQ). The resulting action uses only repeated applications of $Q_{v}$ and shifted positive linear solves, making it compatible with multi-shift Krylov methods. We prove exact preservation of the volume kernel, provide operator-norm and residual error estimates, discuss sector-wise scaling bounds, and validate the method on an embedded $K_{5}$ graph at small spin cutoffs against exact dense local-block operators. Numerical simulations show rapid convergence of vertex expectation values, controlled dependence on bound parameters, and exact preservation of zero-volume modes. We further demonstrate matrix free Monte Carlo estimates at doubled-spin cutoff $2j=250000$ beyond dense materialisation, and show that SRQ can be combined with stochastic Lanczos quadrature to estimate fixed-sector volume spectral measures without dense volume matrices.

</details>


### [3] [Implications of Adler-Finch-Skea solution on charged dark energy star satisfying Karmarkar Condition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18775)
*Pramit Rej*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在爱因斯坦引力框架下，利用Adler-Finch-Skea解和Karmarkar条件构建含各向异性暗能量的带电奇异星模型，并以Her X-1为例验证了模型的无奇点性和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 防止致密天体引力坍缩成奇点，探索暗能量与致密天体的相互作用，构建更简单的带电奇异星模型。

Method: 采用Adler-Finch-Skea解，利用Karmarkar条件确定径向度规分量，Adler方法选择时间度规分量；暗能量采用状态方程建模（暗能量密度与各向同性理想流体物质密度成正比）；通过Darmois-Israel准则平滑匹配确定度规中的未知常数。

Result: 以Her X-1（质量0.85±0.15 M☉，半径8.1 km）为例，所提模型无奇点，满足所有稳定性要求，是一个稳定且物理真实的恒星模型。

Conclusion: 该带电奇异星-暗能量耦合模型在物理一致性和稳定性方面表现良好，可作为防止引力坍缩的可行方案。

Abstract: A possible approach for preventing compact astrophysical objects from gravitational collapse into singularities is the idea of dark energy. Since it is the cause of our universe's accelerated expansion, it has the greatest impact on the cosmos. As a result, it appears that dark energy can interact with any compact astrophysical stellar object [Phys. Rev. D 103, 084042 (2021)]. In this study, our primary objective is to develop a simpler model of a charged strange star coupled with anisotropic dark energy admitting the Adler-Finch-Skea solution [J. Math. Phys. 15, 727 (1974); Class. Quantum Grav. 6, 467 (1989)] within Einstein gravity. To develop this model, the Karmarkar condition was employed to determine the radial metric component, while Adler's methodology was used to choose the time-metric component. For this purpose, we explored a particular strange star, Her X-1, with observed values of mass $(0.85 \pm 0.15)M_{\odot}$ and radius $= 8.1_{-0.41}^{+0.41}$ km. In this context, we proceeded to model dark energy using the equation of state (EoS), such that the density of dark energy is proportional to the density of isotropic perfect fluid matter. The unknown constants in the metric were determined by smooth matching using the Darmois-Israel criterion. We conduct an in-depth examination of the stability and force equilibrium of our suggested star framework, as well as several physical characteristics of the model such as the metric function, pressure, density, mass-radius relation, and dark energy parameters. Thus, the physical consistency and stability of the present model are investigated. Therefore, following a comprehensive theoretical investigation, we discovered that our proposed model is singularity free and meets all the stability requirements to be a stable and physically realistic stellar model.

</details>


### [4] [Non-trivial boundary conditions in general-relativistic models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18868)
*Davide Astesiano,Matteo Luca Ruggiero,Federico Re*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出在广义相对论框架下，通过选择不同的初始和边界条件来解释暗物质效应，认为星系旋转曲线等通常归因于暗物质的现象，实际上可以通过轴对称旋转尘埃流体的自引力系统来重现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战传统暗物质解释，探索在广义相对论框架内通过改变初始和边界条件来替代暗物质假设的可能性。

Method: 从广义相对论出发，研究轴对称旋转尘埃流体构成的自引力系统，通过调整初始条件和边界条件来拟合观测数据。

Result: 证明了典型归因于暗物质（额外物质）的效应，可以通过恰当的初始和边界条件选择来重现，无需引入暗物质。

Conclusion: 暗物质效应可能并非源自实际存在的未知粒子，而是源于对引力系统初始和边界条件设定的不同解释；天文和宇宙学现象的理解依赖于理论框架中的先验假设。

Abstract: We propose an alternative interpretation of dark matter effects within the framework of General Relativity. In particular, we suggest
  that, in astrophysical and cosmological contexts, different initial assumptions about a system inevitably lead to different interpretations of the same phenomena. As a concrete example, we examine self-gravitating systems composed of an axially symmetric rotating dust fluid and show that effects typically attributed to the presence of additional matter, can instead be reproduced through an appropriate choice of initial and boundary conditions for the equations governing the system.

</details>


### [5] [Kiselev black hole and the ultra-slow evaporating behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19110)
*Chen-Hao Wu,Xiao Liang,Ya-Peng Hu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文通过引入动态状态参数$w_q$研究Kiselev黑洞在精质暗能量背景下的蒸发行为，发现$w_q$降低会降低非最终阶段温度并显著延长蒸发寿命，且其超慢蒸发机制与PFDM黑洞和Horndeski黑洞不同，为约束$w_q$值提供了潜在途径，并可能补充宇宙学观测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解精质暗能量背景对黑洞蒸发的影响，特别是通过动态状态参数$w_q$揭示Kiselev黑洞的蒸发特性，并为约束$w_q$值提供理论依据。

Method: 通过引入动态状态参数$w_q$，分析Kiselev黑洞在不同$w_q$取值下的蒸发行为，并与PFDM黑洞和Horndeski黑洞的超慢蒸发机制进行比较。

Result: 发现$w_q$降低会降低黑洞非最终阶段的温度并显著延长蒸发寿命；Kiselev黑洞的超慢蒸发机制与PFDM黑洞和Horndeski黑洞存在本质差异。

Conclusion: 这些结果阐明了动态暗能量背景对黑洞蒸发的影响，为约束$w_q$值提供了潜在实验室，并可补充DESI对退冻暗能量的偏好及基于超慢蒸发的爆炸黑洞观测等宇宙学与天体物理研究。

Abstract: Kiselev solution is a metric that describes black holes immersed in a quintessence-like dark energy background. By introducing a dynamic state parameter $w_q$, the Kiselev solution is supposed to help comprehend the effect of quintessential matter on black holes. In this work, we study the evaporation behaviors of Kiselev black holes. By varying the state parameter $w_q$, we find that the decreasing state parameter lowers the non-final stage temperature and markedly prolongs the evaporation lifetime. We also find that the ultra-slow evaporation mechanism of Kiselev black holes differs vastly from the perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM) black holes and Horndeski black holes, which share the analogous ultra-long lifetime. These results illuminate the effects of dynamic dark energy background on black hole evaporation, provide a potential laboratory to constrain the value of $w_q$, and may complement cosmological and astrophysical observations, e.g., the DESI's preference for thawing dark energy and the observation of exploding black holes based on ultra-slow evaporation.

</details>


### [6] [Impact of the Einstein Telescope's duty cycle on the estimation of binary black holes parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19201)
*Luca Negri,Thomas C. K. Ng,Thibeau Wouters,Tim J. Kuhlbusch,Harsh Narola,Robin Chan,Kailib Ryan Doney,Francesco Cireddu,Isaac C. F. Wong,Fabian Gittins,Peter T. H. Pang,Anuradha Samajdar,Achim Stahl,Justin Janquart,Chris Van Den Broeck,Tjonnie G. F. Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过全贝叶斯参数估计方法，对比了欧洲下一代引力波探测器爱因斯坦望远镜（ET）的两种候选设计方案（三角形ET-Δ与双L形ET-2L），在考虑更精细的占空比模型（连续时间马尔可夫链）和不同维护策略下，发现ET-Δ的冗余设计使其多探测器同时运行时间更长，从而在光度距离和源帧质量等参数约束上优于ET-2L，即使信噪比更低时亦然。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前基于Fisher信息矩阵的ET设计方案比较在单探测器运行（由占空比引起）的近似精度不足，需要更精确的处理方法来评估两种设计的科学性能差异。

Method: 采用全贝叶斯参数估计对双黑洞并合的引力波信号进行模拟，利用连续时间马尔可夫链建模精细占空比，并测试不同探测器维护策略，分别对ET-Δ（嵌套三角形）和ET-2L（两个分离的L形探测器）进行对比分析。

Result: ET-Δ的冗余设计使其在大部分观测时间内至少有两个探测器运行，而ET-2L常限于单探测器；在部分网络运行期间，ET-Δ的性能优于ET-2L；更高的多探测器运行时间转化为对光度距离和源帧质量更紧的约束，即便在ET-Δ中信噪比更低时也是如此。

Conclusion: 在考虑实际占空比影响时，ET-Δ设计相比ET-2L具有显著优势，推荐采用三角形配置以确保更好的科学产出。

Abstract: The geometry of the Einstein Telescope, the proposed next-generation European gravitational-wave observatory, is yet to be finalized. Two competing designs are under consideration: a nested triangular configuration (ET-Δ) and two separated L-shaped detectors (ET-2L). Extensive prior comparisons of ET designs established the scientific landscape using the Fisher-information-matrix formalism and identified that duty-cycle-induced single-detector operation is precisely the regime where this approximation becomes less reliable, underscoring the need for a refined, principled treatment of the duty cycle. In this manuscript, we build on that foundation by revisiting the comparison with full Bayesian parameter estimation of gravitational-wave signals from binary black-hole mergers, projected onto a simulated Einstein Telescope that incorporates a refined duty cycle modelled via continuous-time Markov chains and testing different detector maintenance strategies. We find that the redundancy inherent in the ET-Δ design enables it to maintain at least two operational detectors for the majority of the observing time, whereas the ET-2L configuration is often limited to a single detector. Crucially, we show that, during partial network operation, ET-Δ often outperforms ET-2L, and that the increased multi-detector uptime translates into tighter constraints on the luminosity distance and source-frame component masses. Notably, this remains true even when gravitational-wave events have a lower signal-to-noise ratio in ET-Δ than in ET-2L.

</details>


### [7] [Distinct Near-Horizon Trend of Synchrotron Polarization in Kerr Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19229)
*Yehui Hou,Jiewei Huang,Bin Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发现，在Kerr背景下，同步辐射的线性偏振矢量在近地平线展开时具有独特的解析形式。对于稳态、轴对称、退化的电磁场，偏振图案的领先阶仅依赖于Kerr自旋和源极角，而次领先阶修正则编码了电磁场的几何和旋转结构。近地平线偏振因此为探测旋转黑洞的基本性质和引力-电磁相互作用提供了潜在手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展前人（Hou et al. 2024, Chael et al. 2026）在赤道面和离赤道面上的领先阶分析，推导近地平线偏振矢量的高阶解析形式，以挖掘偏振信号对黑洞基本性质及引力-电磁相互作用的探测潜力。

Method: 在Kerr背景下对同步辐射的线性偏振矢量进行近地平线展开，分别导出领先阶和次领先阶解析形式；领先阶仅与Kerr自旋和源极角相关，次领先阶进一步编码电磁场的几何与旋转结构。

Result: 得到了偏振矢量在近地平线区域的独特解析表达式：领先阶图案由黑洞自旋和极角决定，次领先阶修正包含电磁场结构信息。

Conclusion: 近地平线偏振有望成为探测旋转黑洞基本属性及引力-电磁相互作用的新探针。

Abstract: We show that the near-horizon expansion of the linear polarization vector for synchrotron emission in a Kerr background admits a distinct analytic form. For emission from a stationary, axisymmetric, degenerate electromagnetic field, the leading-order polarization pattern depends only on the Kerr spin and the source polar angle, while the next-to-leading-order correction further encodes the geometric and rotational structure of the electromagnetic field. Our result extends the equatorial analysis of [Hou et al. (2024)] and the off-equatorial leading-order result of [Chael et al. (2026)]. Near-horizon polarization thus offers a potential probe of the fundamental properties of rotating black holes and of gravito-electromagnetic interactions.

</details>


### [8] [A Potential Black Hole Mimicker From Non-Minimal Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19291)
*Debanjan Debnath,Rikpratik Sengupta,Kaushik Bhattacharya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类在曲率-流体耦合引力理论中产生的无视界、规则超紧凑天体。内部由真空态方程驱动，外部为Schwarzschild时空，两者通过一个壳层连接。该模型自然选择了典型的质量-半径窗口（质量1.4-2.1 M⊙，半径5-7 km），并预测了独特的几何热力学壳层温度和与质量无关的光度，可能在不产生事件视界的情况下模拟黑洞现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Mazur-Mottola引力星及其变体模型存在局限性，本文旨在通过曲率-流体耦合机制构建一种无视界的超紧凑天体模型，该模型自然地选择特定的质量-半径窗口，并能模拟黑洞现象，同时提供区别于Hawking辐射的独特观测特征。

Method: 在曲率-流体耦合引力理论中引入流体变量与Ricci标量的非最小相互作用，使内部产生类真空态方程；外部保持标准Schwarzschild解；两个时空区域通过一个壳层连接，壳层获得刚性物质态方程。模型在超紧凑极限下求解壳层的几何热力学温度，并分析其质量-半径关系与观测特征。

Result: 模型自然地选择了质量范围1.4-2.1 M⊙、半径范围5-7 km的超紧凑质量-半径窗口；预测了与Hawking温度截然不同的壳层温度；预言了与质量无关的光度这一独特观测特征。

Conclusion: 该模型在不依赖事件视界的情况下成功模拟了黑洞的紧凑性，同时通过独特的温度和质量无关光度提供了可观测的检验窗口，为区分黑洞与超紧凑天体提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We present a class of horizonless, regular ultra-compact objects arising in a theory of gravity which allows curvature-fluid coupling. The non-minimal interaction between fluid variables and the Ricci scalar generates a vacuum-like equation of state in the interior, while the exterior remains exactly Schwarzschild. The two spacetimes are glued through a shell at the junction. The interior metric is non-singular, the shell acquires a stiff-matter equation of state, and near-horizon compactness can potentially mimic black-hole phenomenology without event horizons. Unlike the Mazur-Mottola gravastar and its variants, the present model naturally selects a typical ultra-compact mass-radius window, with masses in the range $1.4$-$2.1 M_\odot$ and radii in the range 5-7 km. This framework predicts a unique geometric-thermodynamic shell temperature in the ultra-compact limit distinctly different from the Hawking expression and the other unique observational feature of the model is the prediction of mass independent luminosity.

</details>


### [9] [Quantum fate of the Choptuik naked singularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17135)
*Chih-Hung Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 经典临界坍缩中出现的裸奇点会严重破坏可预测性，但本文通过半经典分析表明，量子反作用会消除这种破坏：在2+1维和3+1维模型中，量子效应会在原本裸露的区域上产生一个量子俘获视界或有限质量的边际陷获面，从而将裸奇点覆盖，使其退化为与普通黑洞奇点类似的、仅与蒸发问题相关的可预测性丧失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典临界坍缩中，从光滑初态出发会动力学地形成裸奇点，这比普通黑洞奇点更严重地违反可预测性。本文旨在论证量子反作用能够消除这种差异，从而恢复可预测性。

Method: 在半经典框架下，基于坍缩物质量子自能产生的普适增长模式和有限质量间隙，分别对2+1维和3+1维爱因斯坦-标量系统中的外部裸奇点区域进行受控分析。2+1维中使用光滑匹配和物理边界条件解析选择真空极化态；3+1维中通过数值视界追踪研究量子移位阈值附近的外部演化。

Result: 2+1维中，真空极化的反作用通过量子俘获分支掩盖了经典裸露区域；3+1维中，量子移位阈值附近外部形成有限质量的边际陷获面，而非零质量的裸端点。

Conclusion: 量子效应将假设的柯西视界推至量子生成的视界之后，使得Choptuik裸奇点与普通黑洞奇点面临相同的命运——可预测性的丧失仅降级为标准黑洞蒸发问题。

Abstract: Classical critical collapse provides a dynamical route from smooth initial data to a naked singularity, representing a sharper violation of predictability than ordinary black hole singularities. We argue that this distinction is erased by quantum backreaction. Building on the semiclassical interior analysis, where quantum self-energy of the collapsing matter generates a universal growing mode and a finite mass gap, we study the exterior naked singularity region that determines global visibility in the Einstein-scalar system. We analyze controlled exterior models in both $2+1$ and $3+1$ dimensions. In the former, smooth matching and physical boundary conditions analytically select a vacuum polarization state, whose backreaction cloaks the classically naked region by a quantum trapped branch. In the latter, numerical horizon tracing shows that near a quantum-shifted threshold the exterior develops finite-mass marginally trapped surfaces rather than a zero-mass naked endpoint. These results suggest a global quantum picture in which the Choptuik naked singularity shares the fate of an ordinary black hole singularity: quantum effects push the putative Cauchy horizon behind a quantum-generated horizon, thereby reducing the loss of predictability to the standard black hole evaporation problem.

</details>

Method: 基于帕斯卡型剩余构造方法，在ℙ⁴中构造两组超平面四元组，分析其对偶平面交线的几何性质，利用代数几何方法证明剩余平面位于三次三维簇上。

In the general case this cubic is the Segre cubic, and the construction recovers its fifteen planes and the associated Cremona--Richmond configuration. Abstract: We study the geometry of polynomial neural networks with monomial activation functions and no bias. We introduce a general framework of algebraic networks, together with their realization maps and associated affine neurovarieties. In this setting we define morphisms, subnetworks, symmetry groups and quotient parameter spaces and we discuss geometric notions of identifiability and reducibility.
  Our main goal is to relate the singularities of neurovarieties to degenerations of the underlying architecture. For fully connected networks, we define the architectural degeneracy locus as the locus of functions admitting a representation by parameters with a rank-deficient layer or an inactive hidden neuron. We prove that, for fully connected networks with non-increasing widths and scalar output, full parameters give smooth points of the corresponding neurovariety under explicit layerwise regularity assumptions. In particular, for these architectures, the singular locus is contained in the architectural degeneracy locus.

### [15] [Coincidence Correspondences and Nonlinear Root Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18498)
*Alok Shukla*

Main category: math.AG

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (1) 从有限态射Q: X→Y的自纤维积X×_Y X的非对角不可约分支出发，构造局域对称算子和内蕴Cartan型不变量；(2) 建立秩二约化定理，推导迹与行列式公式，分类为椭圆、抛物、双曲传输类型；(3) 引入传输图册(transport atlases)与联络数据，构造非线性Cartan场。

Conclusion: 经典Weyl与复反射几何是这种基于对应的更广泛根理论的特例，该理论可超越有限反射群的限制。

Abstract: We show that finite morphisms of smooth algebraic varieties naturally give rise to Cartan--Coxeter type structures. Starting from the self-fiber product $X\times_YX$ of a finite morphism $Q:X\to Y$, we construct local symmetry operators and intrinsic Cartan-type invariants from the geometry of its non-diagonal irreducible components. This provides a mechanism for reconstructing root-theoretic structures directly from algebraic correspondences rather than from reflection groups.
  A central part of the theory is a rank-two geometry associated with pairs of non-diagonal components. We establish a rank-two reduction theorem, derive explicit trace and determinant formulas for the corresponding operators, and obtain a classification into elliptic, parabolic, and hyperbolic transport types. These results yield intrinsic analogues of Cartan matrices, Coxeter transformations, exponents, and Dynkin diagrams associated with finite morphisms.
  We further prove rigidity theorems showing that the structures arising from a single finite morphism are highly constrained. To obtain richer geometries, we introduce transport atlases of compatible local finite covers equipped with connection data, leading to nonlinear Cartan fields with variable local geometry. This places classical Weyl and complex reflection geometries within a broader correspondence-based root theory extending beyond finite reflection groups.

### [16] [Isomonodromic deformations, $\mathbb C^*$-actions, and characterization of non-abelian Noether-Lefschetz loci on Dolbeault moduli spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18768)
*Tianzhi Hu,Ruiran Sun,Jinbang Yang,Kang Zuo*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究光滑投影簇的平滑真族上，通过相对非阿贝尔霍奇对应从等单值形变得到的实解析Higgs丛族，证明了其与Dolbeault模空间上C*作用的交互关系，并给出了Simpson非阿贝尔Noether-Lefschetz locus的一个局部刻画的新证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解等单值形变与Dolbeault模空间上自然的C*作用之间的相互作用，并回答Esnault与Kerz提出的关于非阿贝尔Noether-Lefschetz locus的问题。

Method: 基于Higgs丛的实解析形变与调和度量变分的研究，通过分析重新缩放族是否保持等单值性来刻画复解析子簇上σ_Dol的全纯性。

Result: (1) 若σ_Dol|_U是全纯的，则对任意λ∈S^1，重新缩放族λ·σ_Dol|_U仍是等单值的；(2) 若存在λ∈S^1\{±1}使得λ·σ_Dol|_U是等单值的，则σ_Dol|_U必为全纯的。

Conclusion: 给出了HSJZ定理1.2的简化证明：初始局部系统承载极化复Hodge结构的变分时，非阿贝尔Noether-Lefschetz locus恰为σ_Dol成为全纯的最大复解析子簇。

Abstract: Let $f:X\to S$ be a smooth proper family of smooth projective varieties, and let $σ_{\mathrm{Dol}}:\,S \to M_{\mathrm{Dol}}(X/S)$ be the real analytic family of Higgs bundles obtained from an isomonodromic deformation via the relative non-abelian Hodge correspondence. We study the interaction between isomonodromic deformation and the natural $\mathbb C^*$-action on Dolbeault moduli spaces. For $λ\in S^1$, we prove that, on any complex analytic subvariety $U\subset S$, the rescaled family $λ\cdotσ_{\mathrm{Dol}}|_U$ is again isomonodromic if $σ_{\mathrm{Dol}}|_U$ is holomorphic. Conversely, we prove that $σ_{\mathrm{Dol}}|_U$ must be holomorphic if there exists $λ\in S^1\backslash\{\pm 1\}$ such that $λ\cdotσ_{\mathrm{Dol}}|_U$ is isomonodromic. The proof is based on the study of real analytic deformations of Higgs bundles and the variation of harmonic metrics.
  As an application, we give a simplified proof of a local characterization of Simpson's non-abelian Noether--Lefschetz locus firstly proved in \cite[Theorem 1.2]{HSJZ}. Namely, if the initial local system underlies a polarized complex variation of Hodge structures, then the non-abelian Noether--Lefschetz locus is precisely the maximal complex analytic subvariety of $S$ on which the real analytic section $σ_{\mathrm{Dol}}$ becomes holomorphic. This gives an affirmative answer to a question of Esnault and Kerz.

### [17] [A Symmetry Method for Key Vanishing Lemmas and Optimal $2$-Jet Thresholds for Hyperbolicity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19155)
*Tao Cui,Lei Hou,Jianjun Liu,Song-Yan Xie*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于对称性的新方法，通过引入交换两个坐标的对合不变性，结合表示论和C++并行计算，证明了一般三次空间中次数d≥16的非常一般曲面是Kobayashi双曲的，并为达到最优界（d≥15的曲面和d≥11的平面曲线补集）奠定了理论基础。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 使用Fermat型方程的两项摄动，该摄动在交换两个坐标的对合下不变；2) 分析诱导的对合在不变2-jet微分空间上的线性作用；3) 利用Z/2Z表示论的特征向量论证生成额外的线性约束，将欠定系统变为高度超定系统；4) 使用C++实现并行化和模运算求解这些超定系统。

Result: 证明了一般三次空间中次数d≥16的非常一般曲面是Kobayashi双曲的。d=15和d=11的情况计算已在进行中。

Conclusion: 新对称性方法有效解决了此前不可解的约束系统问题，为达到最优双曲性界提供了理论框架。C++代码已完成，剩余情况的计算有望在近期完成。

Abstract: This manuscript reports on an ongoing project. We develop a new symmetry-based method for establishing vanishing results for negatively twisted invariant 2-jet differentials, both on generic surfaces in $\mathbb{P}^3$ and on complements of generic plane curves. The approach improves upon the recent work of Hou--Huynh--Merker--Xie by using a two-term perturbation of Fermat-type equations that is invariant under an involution exchanging two coordinates. The induced linear action on the space of invariant 2-jet differentials, combined with an elementary eigenvector argument from the representation theory of $\mathbb{Z}/2\mathbb{Z}$, generates numerous additional linear constraints. This transforms the previously intractable systems into highly overdetermined ones, which we solve with a C++ implementation incorporating parallelization and modular arithmetic.
  Our ultimate goal is to prove that a very generic surface in $\mathbb{P}^3$ of degree $d \geqslant 15$ is Kobayashi hyperbolic, and that the complement of a generic curve in $\mathbb{P}^2$ of degree $d \geqslant 11$ is hyperbolic. As a concrete step, we prove here that a very generic surface in $\mathbb{P}^3$ of degree $d \geqslant 16$ is Kobayashi hyperbolic. The method developed in this paper also lays the theoretical foundation for the vanishing results needed to reach the optimal bounds. Since many colleagues have asked to see the new symmetry method, we are making this manuscript available now. The C++ code for the remaining cases $d=15$ and $d=11$ is already written and the computations are underway; we expect to complete them in the near future.

Motivation: 研究代数锥乘积上的全纯张量在收缩作用下的不变性，并探索Sasaki流形几何结构中的类似性质。

Method: 先证明代数锥乘积商空间上的全纯张量在Zariski闭包下的不变性，再通过构造Sasaki流形锥到正规簇的显式嵌入，结合前一部分结果推导出Sasaki流形乘积上全纯张量在Reeb场流下的不变性。

Result: 证明了两个代数锥乘积商空间上的全纯张量在收缩的Zariski闭包下不变，以及Sasaki流形乘积上的全纯张量在Reeb场流下不变。

Conclusion: 建立了代数锥几何与Sasaki几何之间的桥梁，揭示了全纯张量在不同几何结构中的不变性规律。

Abstract: We study the product $C$ of two algebraic cones equipped with algebraic structures given by contractions. First we show that any holomorphic tensor on a quotient of $C$ by a group containing a contraction on both factors is invariant under the Zariski closure of this contraction when the factors have dimension $\geq 2$. We then give an explicit embedding of the cone of a Sasaki manifold to a normal variety. Using it and the result on algebraic cones, we prove that any holomorphic tensor on the product of two Sasaki manifolds is invariant under the flows of the Reeb fields.

### [21] [Persistent Entropy of Floer Persistence Barcodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19071)
*Wenmin Gong*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种新的Floer理论不变量——持久熵（persistent entropy），它是基于条形码长度分布Shannon熵的渐近线性增长率，证明了与条形码熵的等价关系，并建立了与测地流拓扑熵的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受拓扑数据分析中持久条形码Shannon熵的启发，为Floer同调引入一个互补于条形码熵的新的熵不变量，以量化条形码长度分布的线性增长信息。

Method: 定义持久熵为迭代下有限条形码长度分布Shannon熵的渐近线性增长率；通过比较相对/绝对持久熵与条形码熵的关系进行理论分析；利用Liouville域的比较不等式和次指数长度增长准则推导等式条件；计算余切圆盘丛的持久熵并与测地流拓扑熵关联；证明Hofer稳定性估计。

Result: 对Hamilton微分同胚，相对与绝对持久熵分别与相应条形码熵一致；对Liouville域，建立了一般比较不等式及次指数长度增长准则下的等式条件（超越平凡辛同调情形）；负曲率流形余切圆盘丛的持久熵等于测地流拓扑熵；建立了有限层Shannon熵的Hofer稳定性估计。

Conclusion: 持久熵是Floer理论中一个与条形码熵互补但等价的新不变量，能够捕捉动力学与几何信息（如测地流拓扑熵），并为Reeb流的刚性与柔性现象提供了分析工具。

Abstract: Floer persistence barcodes provide a quantitative way to encode action-filtered Floer homology. Inspired by the Shannon entropy of persistence barcodes in topological data analysis, we introduce a Floer-theoretic entropy invariant, called \textit{persistent entropy}, which measures the asymptotic linear growth rate, under iteration, of the Shannon entropy determined by the distribution of finite bar lengths. This is complementary to the barcode entropy of Çineli--Ginzburg--Gürel, which records the exponential growth rate of the number of not-too-short bars. We prove that, for Hamiltonian diffeomorphisms, the relative and absolute persistent entropies coincide with the corresponding barcode entropies. For Liouville domains, we prove general comparison inequalities and a subexponential length-growth criterion which gives equality beyond the case of vanishing symplectic homology. We also compute the persistent entropy of cotangent disk bundles of negatively curved manifolds and relate it to the topological entropy of the geodesic flow. In addition, we prove Hofer-stability estimates for finite-level Shannon entropy and derive flexibility and rigidity-type questions for barcode and persistent entropies of Reeb flows.

</details>

### [27] [Ghosts versus Unstable Particles in Quantum Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18349)
*Luca Buoninfante*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过对比鬼粒子与不稳定粒子的解析结构差异，阐明了阈值以上鬼粒子的物理本质：鬼粒子传播子的共轭复极点位于第一黎曼面，导致其渐近存活但不具有粒子解释；有限时间效应会放大共振行为差异，支持渐近极限下不存在自由传播鬼粒子的结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阐明多粒子阈值以上鬼粒子的物理本质，通过对比量子场论中鬼粒子与不稳定粒子的根本区别，解决鬼粒子是否具有可观测物理效应以及能否作为自由传播粒子的核心问题。

Method: 首先从渐近公式出发，分析正规化传播子的解析结构（极点所在黎曼面）；然后构建有限时间区间的量子场论，在适当的传播子近似下研究有限时间效应对共振行为的影响，并识别不同时间区间的动力学特征。

Result: 鬼粒子传播子的共轭复极点位于第一黎曼面（普通不稳定粒子位于第二黎曼面）；鬼共振更窄，正负能量峰之间干涉更弱；有限时间效应进一步放大差异并产生新特征（如更高的共振峰）；表明渐近极限下不存在自由传播的鬼粒子。

Conclusion: 鬼粒子与不稳定粒子在解析结构上存在根本性区别，前者在渐近极限下无法作为自由传播粒子存在，支持了其非粒子性的物理本质；有限时间效应为实验区分鬼共振与普通共振提供了新的可能。

Abstract: We elucidate the physical nature of ghosts above the multi-particle threshold by contrasting them with unstable particles in quantum field theory. We first consider the asymptotic formulation, where ordinary positive-norm one-particle states can be unstable and decay, whereas ghosts survive asymptotically without decaying, yet admit no particle interpretation due to interference with the multi-particle component which masks the negative-norm one-particle state. This distinction originates from two different analytic structures of the dressed propagator, whose complex conjugate poles lie in the first or second Riemann sheet in the ghost or ordinary case, respectively. Ghost resonances are, in principle, phenomenologically distinguishable from ordinary ones, being narrower and exhibiting weaker interference between positive- and negative-energy peaks. We then formulate the quantum field theory in a finite interval of time and, working within a suitable approximation for the dressed propagator, find that finite-time effects amplify differences in the resonant behavior and give rise to new features, such as higher peaks in ghost resonances. Distinct temporal regimes are also identified: for times shorter than the inverse width, an approximate free-particle description is valid, whereas at later times interactions and interference effects dominate, leading to decay or multi-particle masking. Complex poles in the dressed propagator emerge only at late times and become complex-conjugate pairs asymptotically, determining the asymptotic dynamics. This study supports the absence of freely propagating ghost particles in the asymptotic limit.

Abstract: Ordinary, s-wave superconductors have been recognized as being topological phases of matter, in which the dynamical gauge field implies less understood global features. Using the tools of topological field theories and generalized symmetries, we provide an updated description of these systems. At very low energies, the Higgs model reduces to the BF theory, which exhibits topological order. Furthermore, the gauge field must be a spin$_c$ connection, to describe the spin of fermions forming Cooper pairs. Gauging implies that superconductors are inherently bosonic systems, yet they are endowed with a gravito-magnetic anomaly that is the remnant of their fermionic origin. We recognize that this anomaly is related to the Gaiotto-Kapustin-Thorngren bosonization, achieved via gauging fermion parity $(-1)^F$, now included in the gauge dynamics. This anomaly characterizes gauged electronic matter in great generality in three and four spacetime dimensions, forbidding trivial massive phases at low energy. It holds beyond the validity of the Higgs model, nd in other kinds of superconductors as well. It also appears in the nontrivial massless phase of three-dimensional electrodynamics, recently understood.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在可积的一圈极限和预期的全圈可积性之间，研究有限圈截断中混沌行为如何涌现，探究过渡区间的量子混沌特征。

Method: 使用谱统计（能级间距分布）、本征矢量诊断（随机矩阵比较）和扩展复杂性（Krylov空间分析）三种方法系统分析有限圈截断的混沌特征。

Result: 二圈和四圈截断在足够大耦合下呈现GOE统计但弱可积性破坏特征；四圈可积性破坏比二圈更弱，临界耦合更大；三圈未见混沌；本征态随机性弱于GOE；Krylov空间数据与谱统计相关。

Conclusion: 有限圈膨胀算子并非一般长程自旋链哈密顿量，其混沌模式与全圈平面理论可积性恢复一致，暗示了可积性在微扰展开中的某种保护机制。

Abstract: We study signatures of quantum chaos in finite-loop truncations of the planar dilatation operator in the $\mathfrak{su}(2)$ sector of $\mathcal N=4$ super Yang-Mills and its $β$-deformation. These truncations define holographically motivated long-range deformations of the nearest-neighbour XXX spin chain. At one-loop the model is integrable, while the all-loop planar theory is expected to again be integrable. Finite-loop truncations therefore provide a natural setting for investigating how chaotic behaviour emerges between these two integrable limits. We analyse this question using spectral statistics, eigenvector diagnostics and spread complexity. We find that the two- and four-loop truncations develop GOE-like level statistics at sufficiently large coupling but with features characteristic of weak integrability breaking. The integrability breaking at four-loops is weaker than at two-loops and the critical coupling at which chaos occurs is larger, at least for long spin chains. The three-loop truncation does not show the same onset of chaos in the range studied. Eigenvector diagnostics show that the corresponding eigenstates remain less random than GOE vectors, indicating weak ergodicity and multifractality. Finally, we can identify signatures of the eigenvalue and eigenvector chaos in the Krylov-space data. Namely, we demonstrate a correlation of the level spacing statistics with the peak of spread complexity and disorder on the Krylov chain. The delocalisation of the initial state in the Hamiltonian eigenbasis is shown to strongly affect the saturation of complexity. Our results suggest that finite-loop dilatation operators are not generic long-range spin chain Hamiltonians, but already display patterns consistent with the restoration of integrability in the all-loop planar theory.

</details>


### [30] [Tracing Transcendentality in Protected Correlators of N=4 SYM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18362)
*Marco S. Bianchi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了N=4 SYM理论中受保护标量算符的两点函数，重点分析了维数约化下的超越性性质。通过双圈图和最高经典维数10的具体计算，发现单圈修正具有普适性，而双圈图修正中高维算符的均匀超越性出现可控的部分破缺，可通过可预测的方式消除。主要结果是得到了任意维数和迹结构的双圈关联函数的完整平面外推，其依赖性完全由算符中应力张量多重态因子数量控制，并与局域化预言相符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索N=4 SYM中受保护标量算符两点函数在维数约化框架下的超越性行为，特别是高维算符是否保持均匀超越性，以及如何系统描述和修正超越性破缺现象。

Method: 采用微扰计算方法，具体计算到双圈阶，算符经典维数最高至10，涵盖所有迹结构。通过维数约化技术处理正则子，分析单圈和双圈修正的超越性特征。

Result: 单圈修正具有普适性。双圈阶下，高维算符出现可控的均匀超越性部分破缺，但可通过特定组合完全抵消。获得了适用于任意维数和迹结构的平面外推公式，其形式由算符中应力张量多重态因子数量唯一确定。

Conclusion: 受保护标量算符的两点函数在微扰层次上展现出丰富的超越性结构，但超越性破缺是完全可控且可预测的。结果与局域化方法的预言在所有可比对情形下一致，验证了计算的正确性。

Abstract: We study two-point functions of protected scalar operators in N=4 SYM, focusing on their transcendentality properties in dimensional reduction, where quantum corrections are subleading in the regulator. We compute the correlators explicitly through two loops and operators up to classical dimension 10, for all trace structures. The one-loop correction is universal. At two loops, we find a controlled partial breaking of uniform transcendentality for higher-dimensional operators, which can be cancelled by suitable combinations of correlators in a fully predictable way. A main result is a complete planar extrapolation for two-loop correlators at arbitrary dimension and trace structure, whose dependence is entirely controlled by the number of stress-tensor multiplet factors in the operator. The perturbative results agree with localization predictions in all cases where comparisons are possible.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用自旋配边群Ω₃^(spin)(BZ₂×X)计算混合全局反常（涉及(-1)^(F_L)与目标空间背景场），识别GSO投影世界面理论的配边类，并推广至一般orbifold [X̂/G] 情形，同时分类所有可能的θ角对应的背景场。

Abstract: Type II string theory in the absence of orientifolds requires the target spacetime $X$ to admit a spin structure. We show that this familiar requirement arises directly from the consistency of the worldsheet GSO projection. The obstruction is a mixed global anomaly between $(-1)^{\text{F}_L}$ and the target space background data, detected by the spin bordism group $Ω_3^{\mathrm{spin}}(B\mathbb{Z}_2\times X)$. We compute the relevant mixed bordism group and identify the bordism class of the GSO-projected worldsheet theory. For smooth target spaces, vanishing of the anomaly reduces to the condition that $X$ is spin, while for general orbifolds $[\hat{X}/G]$, $\hat{X}$ has to carry a $G$-equivariant spin structure. We also classify all possible theta angles in the worldsheet theory and show that they correspond to all possible continuous and discrete background fields of the target space theory visible in string perturbation theory.

### [32] [An effective field theory approach to the sign problem in BFSS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18396)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 符号问题是经典模拟带费米子量子理论的主要障碍，现有方法难以有效处理该问题，亟需新的分析框架。

Method: 提出有效场论方法：在高温下，d+1维场论约化为d维玻色子理论，高维理论中Pfaffian的相位编码在低维理论的一个算符中。将该框架应用于D0-膜/BFSS矩阵量子力学，相位变为玻色子多矩阵积分中的一个算符。

Result: 连续理论在't Hooft大N区域存在符号问题，但该问题的检测需要高溫展開到10圈阶；Pfaffian相位变换为O(9)赝标量；相关图有数值小的前因子；在温度T ≳ λ^{1/3}时忽略符号问题导致的分数误差较小；在't Hooft区域强耦合下符号问题可能更严重。

Conclusion: 高温下符号问题的延迟出现源于Pfaffian相位的对称性性质，在中等耦合温度区域符号问题可忽略，但强耦合下需谨慎处理。

Abstract: The sign problem is a notorious obstacle for classically simulating quantum theories with fermions. We propose an effective field theory method for analyzing the sign problem. At high temperatures, a $d$+1 dimensional field theory reduces to a bosonic $d$-dimensional theory; the phase of the Pfaffian in the higher dimensional theory is encoded in an operator in the lower dimensional theory. We apply this framework to the D0-brane/BFSS matrix quantum mechanics, where the phase becomes an operator in a bosonic multi-matrix integral. Our results show that the continuum theory has a sign problem that persists in the large-$N$ 't Hooft regime. However, detecting the sign problem involves going to 10-loop order in the high-temperature expansion. This delayed onset follows from the fact that the Pfaffian phase transforms as an $O(9)$ pseudoscalar. Furthermore, the relevant diagrams give a numerically small prefactor. Consequently, ignoring the sign problem leads to a relatively small fractional error in thermodynamic quantities for temperatures $T \gtrsim λ^{1/3}$. However, at stronger coupling in the 't Hooft regime, the sign problem may become more severe. Finally, we initiate the application of this framework to higher-dimensional maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theories.

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic stability and the stochastic thermal fluctuations of the warped black hole solution in three-dimensional General Massive Gravity. Going beyond the classical stability analysis, we study thermal fluctuations within a modified finite-time nonequilibrium extension of Ruppeiner's Hessian-based fluctuation theory. For a class of isentropic and isoenergetic processes, we derive exact on-shell angular momentum trajectories in the thermodynamic state space and compute the corresponding thermodynamic lengths. These quantities characterize relaxation processes between macrostates and provide an estimate of the associated relaxation times. Furthermore, we show that the thermodynamic geodesic equations do not admit constant-angular-momentum solutions, suggesting a continuous change of the black hole's angular momentum. Abstract: Color graphs and their subgraphs, referred to as bubble graphs, correspond bijectively to the simplicial complexes of pseudomanifolds and their subsimplices, respectively. In this paper, we introduce matrix representations for colored graphs and their associated bubble graphs. By using this correspondence, we define simplicial-complex matrices and subsimplex matrices that encode the simplicial complexes of pseudomanifolds and their subsimplices. Moreover, we formulate mutation and crossover operations on colored graphs. Through the established correspondence among simplicial complexes, colored graphs, and simplicial-complex matrices, we extend these operations to simplicial complexes and simplicial-complex matrices. We further implement an algorithm generating simplicial-complex matrices and a genetic algorithm performing mutation and crossover of them to produce pseudomanifolds exhibiting diverse topologies. In addition, we implement procedures for decomposing the generated simplicial-complex matrices into simplex matrices, reconstructing the simplicial complexes of the associated pseudomanifolds from this information, and computing geometric quantities such as the volume, circumcenter, and dual-simplex volume of each simplex.

Method: 采用赝厄米共轭定义场伴算符以规避自旋统计定理；使用超场形式（Grassmann奇超场）实现超对称性的显式表达；通过将赝厄米Wess-Zumino模型与厄米Wess-Zumino模型耦合来构造非零三次相互作用。

Abstract: In this work, we construct the simplest pseudo-Hermitian quantum field theory that is supersymmetric. This is the pseudo-Hermitian Wess-Zumino model in the sense that it contains a pair of symplectic fermions (anti-commuting scalar fields) that satisfy the Klein-Gordon equation and a spin-half boson that satisfies the Dirac equation. The conventional spin-statistics theorem is circumvented through the use of pseudo-Hermitian conjugation to define field adjoints. To make the supersymmetry manifest, we formulate the pseudo-Hermitian Wess-Zumino model using the superfield formalism. These superfields are Grassmann-odd so it is not possible to construct non-vanishing cubic interactions using only these superfields. Method: 论文采用路径积分方法分析带有矢量和轴矢量背景规范场的狄拉克费米子，在存在残余无关流-流相互作用的条件下，于红外极限附近进行费米子积分，得到由流表达的半经典低能有效作用量。

Abstract: The path integral of the Dirac fermion with vector and axial gauge backgrounds is analyzed near the infrared limit in the presence of residual irrelevant current-current interaction. After integrating out fermions, a semiclassical low-energy effective action is obtained, written in terms of currents. Its expression is found to correspond to the hydrodynamic action previously proposed for perfect barotropic fluids with anomalies at zero temperature. This approach also leads to two further hydrodynamic actions to be associated, respectively, with the Weyl fermion, and the Dirac fermion having independent vector and axial currents. These actions feature four- and five-dimensional bulk-boundary terms, owing to anomaly inflow, which are identified as being the so-called transgression forms. These are generalizations of Chern--Simons forms that involve two gauge fields: the dynamical field and the background field. The path-integral argument provides a ``microscopic'' explanation for several ingredients of the action formulation of hydrodynamics that are necessary to incorporate anomalies. It also clarifies the infrared reduction required to pass from the effective field theory to a local hydrodynamic description. This reduction is implemented by considering restricted variations of the action, familiar from hydrodynamics, which at the same time lead to four-dimensional equations of motion from the five-dimensional transgression terms.

Abstract: We prove a `nonlinear graviton theorem' for higher-spin self-dual gravity. We show that this space is an infinite dimensional complex manifold with a canonical projection onto a four-dimensional holomorphic self-dual spacetime $\mathcal{M}$, and discuss the geometry induced on this new higher-spin space. Solutions of higher-spin self-dual gravity are then obtained by choosing an embedding of spacetime $\mathcal{M}$ into higher-spin space $M_{HS}$, with higher-spin symmetries arising from the different choices of embedding. Integrability of the theory is manifested in the form of a Lax pair for the system that we present. ### [44] [Universal Closed Form for Dynamical Love Numbers of Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19281)
*Mikhail P. Solon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文推导了Schwarzschild黑洞在所有阶数、所有自旋和多极矩下的动力学响应Love数的闭式解析表达式，揭示了其因子化结构源于硬匹配系数、近区反常维度和远区重整化对数的披饰，并通过壳层有效场论验证至$\mathcal O(G^{15})$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态黑洞Love数为零，但动力学Love数非零，此前缺乏闭式解析解。本文旨在给出Schwarzschild黑洞动力学响应的普适闭式公式，并揭示其物理根源与因子化结构。

Method: 方法包括：(1) 利用重整化群方程求解近区对数解$\Phi_{\ell,s}$，并将运行对数$\tau$通过对Riemann zeta值的无穷求和披饰至全阶；(2) 识别出该zeta级数源于远区$Γ(1-η)$的Newton相移，具有跨多极矩和自旋的普适性；(3) 因子化框架：硬匹配系数(视界) × 反常维度(近区) × 披饰对数(远区)；(4) 壳层有效场论独立验证标量、电磁和引力扰动。

Result: 闭式结果：$\bar{F}_{\ell,s}/4πR_S^{2\ell+1}=Φ_{\ell,s}(\bar{y})-\tfrac12η\,Φ_{\ell,s}'(\bar{y})$，其中$\bar{y}=-\tfrac12η^2τ$，$η=iωR_S$，$τ=\log(R_S/R)-2\sum_{k\ge2}ζ_k\,η^{k-1}$。该公式对所有自旋$s$和多极矩$\ell$成立，经壳层EFT验证至$\mathcal O(G^{15})$。

Conclusion: 动力学Love数可解析计算至全阶，其核心结构由三个独立成分因子化构成；Riemann zeta级数的出现揭示了Newton相移与黑洞响应之间的深层联系，为引力波物理和黑洞微扰理论提供了精确工具。

Abstract: Black hole static Love numbers vanish, but their dynamical counterparts do not. We present the scheme-independent dynamical response $\bar{F}_{\ell,s}$ of a Schwarzschild black hole in closed form, to all orders, and for every spin $s$ and multipole $\ell$. The result is $\bar{F}_{\ell,s}/4πR_S^{2\ell+1}=Φ_{\ell,s}(\bar{y})-\tfrac12η\,Φ_{\ell,s}'(\bar{y})$ with $\bar{y}=-\tfrac12η^2τ$ and $η=iωR_S$. Here $Φ_{\ell,s}$ is simply the leading-log solution to the renormalization group equation, but lifting the running logarithm to $τ=\log(R_S/R)-2\sum_{k\ge2}ζ_k\,η^{k-1}$ resums it to all orders. This tower of Riemann zeta values is the Newtonian phase in disguise: it originates from the same far-zone $Γ(1-η)$ that governs long-range scattering, and is universal across multipole and spin. Our result exhibits a factorization pinned to three ingredients: the hard matching coefficient at the horizon, the anomalous dimension in the near zone, and the dressed log in the far zone. Using shell effective field theory, we independently verify our formula for scalar, electromagnetic, and gravitational perturbations, reaching $\mathcal O(G^{15})$.

### [46] [Spectral Functions of Lorentzian Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19321)

TL;DR: 本文在洛伦兹量子引力中计算了引力子模式的谱函数，展示了从经典广义相对论到渐近安全紫外固定点的插值行为。通过使用适用于洛伦兹号型的泛函重整化方法，并结合新的对称性条件以体现 Ward 恒等式，推导并求解了传播子的 Källén-Lehmann 表示的直接流方程。多个重整化条件集合得到一致结果，引力子和标量引力子模式均具有可归一化的谱函数，与红外有效理论一致。进一步计算了曲率二次阶的完整量子有效作用量，提取了引力子诱导的形状因子，并讨论了量子引力幺正性的含义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子引力研究中，理解引力子谱函数在从红外（经典广义相对论）到紫外（渐近安全固定点）整个能标范围内的行为至关重要，这直接关系到理论的幺正性和可重整化性质。然而，在洛伦兹号型下直接计算谱函数面临技术挑战，现有方法多局限于欧几里得号型或微扰框架。

Method: 采用适用于洛伦兹号型的泛函重整化群方法，引入新的对称性条件以强制执行 Ward 恒等式，直接对传播子的 Källén-Lehmann 谱表示建立并求解流方程。通过多个不同的重整化条件设置检验结果的一致性。最终计算了完整量子有效作用量至曲率二次阶，并提取了引力子诱导的形状因子。

Abstract: We compute spectral functions of graviton modes in Lorentzian quantum gravity, interpolating between classical general relativity and an asymptotically safe ultraviolet fixed point. Using functional renormalisation adapted for theories in Lorentzian signature, and enhanced by new symmetry conditions to account for underlying Ward identities, we derive and solve flow equations directly for the Källén-Lehmann representation of propagators. Consistent results are found for several sets of renormalisation conditions yielding normalisable spectral functions for the graviton and the scalar graviton mode, in agreement with effective theory in the infrared. We further calculate the full quantum effective action to quadratic order in curvature, extract graviton-induced form factors, and discuss implications for unitarity of quantum gravity.

</details>

Conclusion: 全息方法能有效描述强耦合下一级逆相变动力学，两种相变表现出不同的动力学特征，退禁闭相变因自由度跳跃大导致气泡壁运动缓慢，手征相变则可通过稳态近似定量分析。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of first-order inverse phase transitions (driven by superheating) at strong coupling, focusing on the top-down Witten-Sakai-Sugimoto model for holographic QCD. Two cases are considered: the deconfinement transition in the unflavored version of the model and a chiral symmetry-restoring transition occurring in the deconfined phase of the full theory. In both cases, we imagine driving the system into a metastable phase at high temperature, inducing the nucleation of bubbles of the stable phase. For both classes of transitions, we find the corresponding Euclidean bounce solutions and compute the bubble nucleation rates and the relevant transition parameters. For the deconfinement transition, the large jump in the number of degrees of freedom between the two phases suggests that the bubble wall velocity is parametrically small; we provide a rough estimate of it near the critical temperature. In the case of the chiral transition, instead, we compute the bubble wall velocity and the friction force exerted on the bubbles employing motivated ansatze and approximations for the steady-state configurations.

*Yongjun Xu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用色散S矩阵自举方法，施加解析性、交叉对称性、分波幺正性和Regge有界性约束，推导出色散关系和交叉零约束；引入Virasoro启发的非线性关系作为额外约束；并采用引力极点减除的正则化方案处理前向极限。

Result: 非线性约束显著缩小了Wilson系数的允许参数区域；在引力极点减除设置下，允许区域被压缩至包含Virasoro-Shapiro点的一个小岛。

Conclusion: Virasoro-Shapiro振幅在低能有效理论参数空间中具有独特的自举特性，非线性约束对其高度确定，为弦理论振幅的唯一性提供了自举层面的解析解释。

Abstract: We study the closed-string tree-level Virasoro-Shapiro amplitude using the dispersive S-matrix bootstrap. For the ten-dimensional maximally supersymmetric four-point amplitude, we impose analyticity, crossing symmetry, partial-wave unitarity, and Regge boundedness. With the massless graviton pole kept explicitly, the resulting dispersion relations and crossing null constraints give numerical bounds on the leading low-energy coefficients normalized by the gravitational coupling. We then introduce a Virasoro-inspired ansatz, which becomes a set of nonlinear relations among Wilson coefficients and shrinks the allowed region toward the Virasoro-Shapiro trajectory. Finally, we study a gravity-pole-subtracted setup, where the regular part of the amplitude has a well-defined forward limit. In this stripped problem, the nonlinear constraints reduce the allowed region to a small island containing the Virasoro-Shapiro point, for which we provide an analytic bootstrap explanation.

</details>

### [50] [Light pillars over rippled water: why their sides appear parallel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18547)
*Philip W. Kuchel*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个几何光学模型，解释了水面波纹产生的光柱现象：水面微小面元作为反射镜，其物理宽度随距离增加而扩大，但透视投影的压缩效应恰好抵消这一扩大，导致光柱在图像中宽度恒定。这是首次对该现象的正式学术记录。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 波纹水面上的路灯反射常呈现高大、狭窄且两侧平行的光柱，视觉效果类似建筑结构，但水面既非垂直也非光滑。此前缺乏对这一日常视觉现象的系统性物理解释，定性分析也未考虑投影几何的关键作用。

Method: 建立几何光学模型，将波纹水面视为微小面元（波上的切平面）组成的反射镜阵列。结合镜面反射定律、投影几何及水面斜率的物理统计特性，分析从远处看向水面时，反射光线进入眼睛/相机（针孔）的几何关系。

Result: 发现两个效应相互抵消：随着观察距离（x）增加，反射光进入眼睛的水面物理区域宽度增大；但针孔投影到像平面时，该宽度被1/x因子压缩。两者精确抵消，使得光柱在图像中的宽度恒定。模型还解释了光柱两端的偏差、亮度变化及扩展物体（如建筑物）不产生拉长反射的原因。

Conclusion: 该框架可自然推广至更复杂的观察场景（如悬崖上看海面落日）。面向初等光学学者及对日常视觉现象物理机制感兴趣的读者。

Abstract: Streetlights shining across rippled water often produce tall, narrow reflections with strikingly parallel sides. These light pillars appear almost architectural, yet the water surface is neither vertical nor smooth. We develop a geometric optics model that explains the phenomenon using the specular reflection rule, projection geometry, and the physics and statistics of surface slopes. A rippled water surface can be viewed as an ensemble of small facets (tangent planes on waves) acting as tiny mirrors. As one looks farther across the water (coordinate x), the physical width of the region whose facets reflect the light into the eye (or camera/pinhole) increases, but the pinhole projection onto the image plane compresses this widening by a factor proportional to 1/x. The two effects cancel, producing a reflection whose image width remains constant. This paper appears to be the first to formally document this. (Deviations from the strict cancellation at both ends of the image are also explained.) The analysis clarifies how earlier qualitative treatments failed through a lack of identifying the role of projection geometry. The model also qualitatively explains the brightness variation along the pillar, and why extended objects such as buildings do not produce elongated reflections. The treatment is intended for scholars of introductory optics and for those interested in the physics and mathematics of everyday visual phenomena. We conclude by outlining how the same framework extends naturally to more complex viewing situations, such as the setting sun viewed from a cliff top over the sea.

</details>

*Ravindra Singh*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文通过广义δ-不变量，建立了黎曼浸没和黎曼映射的广义B.-Y. Chen不等式，得到了最优不等式并刻画了等式成立的条件，推广了经典Chen不等式及现有相关结果。

Method: 采用广义δ-不变量，结合垂直分布和水平分布的外在不变量（由第二基本张量决定），通过形状算子上的精确代数条件刻画等式情形并给出几何解释。

Result: 得到了黎曼浸没和黎曼映射的最优广义Chen不等式，并在总空间或目标空间为实空间形式和复空间形式时得到了显式不等式。

Abstract: In this paper, we establish generalized B.-Y. Chen inequalities for Riemannian submersions and Riemannian maps between Riemannian manifolds by employing the generalized $δ$-invariants introduced by Chen. We derive optimal inequalities involving the generalized $δ$-invariants associated with the vertical and horizontal distributions together with extrinsic invariants determined by the second fundamental tensors of the submersion and the Riemannian map. Furthermore, we characterize the equality cases through precise algebraic conditions on the corresponding shape operators, providing their geometric interpretation. As applications, we obtain explicit generalized Chen inequalities for Riemannian submersions and Riemannian maps whose total or target manifolds are real space forms and complex space forms. These results extend the classical Chen inequalities as well as several recent Chen-type inequalities for Riemannian submersions and Riemannian maps available in the literature.

*Liam Mazurowski,Xuan Yao*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Further assume that $g$ can be uniformly approximated on compact sets by smooth metrics with almost non-negative scalar curvature. For such a metric $g$, we define a synthetic ADM mass $m(g)$ using harmonic functions. The harmonic mass $m(g)$ coincides with the usual ADM mass whenever $g$ is smooth and decays rapidly enough that the latter is defined. The harmonic mass can also be computed as a limit of the $C^0$ local mass introduced by Burkhardt-Guim. Our main result is a positive mass theorem: the harmonic mass satisfies $m(g)\geq 0$ and if $m(g) = 0$ then $g$ is flat.

### [57] [Diffeomorphic Logarithm of Special Orthogonal Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19223)
*Zhifeng Deng,P. -A. Absil,Kyle A. Gallivan,Wen Huang*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文刻画了特殊正交群 SO_n 上指数映射的局部微分同胚结构，发现了包含主对数的区域具有至多两个原像的特殊重数性质，并据此提出了一种高效稳定的微分同胚对数算法，该算法在 Karcher 均值问题中展现出比主对数更好的连续性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SO_n 上的指数映射及其逆问题（矩阵对数）具有高度非平凡的局部微分同胚结构，现有研究对此结构认识不足，且主对数存在不连续性，难以满足某些应用场景（如Karcher均值）的需求。

Method: 利用 Schur 分解的规范对齐（canonical alignment）方法，将导数可逆的斜对称矩阵集合组织成微分同胚的区域，并研究各区域的结构性质；基于该几何框架构造微分同胚对数算法。

Result: 揭示了包含主对数的区域具有特殊的重数结构：SO_n 中每个矩阵在该区域至多有两个斜对称原像；提出的微分同胚对数算法高效且稳定；在 Karcher 均值问题中，该对数生成的均值在数据扰动下具有连续行为，而主对数无法实现这一性质。

Conclusion: 本文建立的微分同胚对数框架为 SO_n 上的几何计算提供了更优的工具，尤其在对连续性有要求的应用中（如均值问题）优于传统的基于主对数的方法。

Abstract: The special orthogonal group $\mathbb{SO}_n$ is a Lie group whose geometry and local structure are encoded by the exponential map in its Lie algebra $\mathbf{Skew}_n$, the set of skew-symmetric matrices. The associated multi-valued inverse problem -- the matrix logarithm -- in $\mathbb{SO}_n$ exhibits a highly nontrivial local diffeomorphism structure, which differs from the matrix logarithm for invertible matrices. This work characterizes the local diffeomorphism structure of the exponential in the set of skew-symmetric matrices where its derivative is invertible. We show that this set with an invertible derivative can be organized into diffeomorphic regions, using a canonical alignment of Schur decompositions. In particular, the region that contains the principal logarithm has a special multiplicity structure: each matrix in $\mathbb{SO}_n$ admits at most two skew-symmetric preimages in this region. Based on this geometric framework, we introduce the diffeomorphic logarithm of special orthogonal matrices together with an efficient and stable algorithm. Moreover, it is applied to the Karcher mean problem in $\mathbb{SO}_n$, demonstrating continuous behavior of the mean under perturbations of the data, which is not captured by the principal logarithm.

</details>


### [58] [Cohomogeneity one actions on symmetric spaces of mixed type](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19323)
*Tomas Otero,Ivan Solonenko,Hiroshi Tamaru*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了混合型对称空间上的等距余齐度一作用，发现了一类新的"对角"作用，并证明了除这类作用外，任何余齐度一作用都可分解为各因子上的等距作用之积，从而将分类问题简化为单一类型对称空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将余齐度一作用的分类问题从混合型对称空间约化到单一类型（紧致、非紧致、欧几里得型）对称空间，填补混合型对称空间中该问题的研究空白。

Method: 通过分析混合型对称空间的几何结构，构造了一类新的"对角"余齐度一作用，并证明了其余作用均可分解为各因子的等距作用之积。

Result: 发现了一族新的对角型余齐度一作用（作用于 $\mathbb{R}^n \times M_-$ 形式的空间），并证明了除该族作用外，任何余齐度一作用都分解为紧致、欧几里得和非紧致因子上的等距作用之积。

Conclusion: 余齐度一作用的分类问题可完全约化到单一类型对称空间（紧致、非紧致或欧几里得型）上进行研究，混合型空间上仅存在一个特殊例外族。

Abstract: In this article, we study isometric cohomogeneity-one actions on symmetric spaces of mixed type, i.e., those whose universal cover splits as a nontrivial product of symmetric spaces of compact, noncompact, and Euclidean types. We provide a new family of "diagonal" cohomogeneity-one actions on symmetric spaces of the form $\mathbb{R}^n \times M_-$, where $M_-$ is of noncompact type. We show that, with the exception of this family, any cohomogeneity-one action on a symmetric space decomposes as a product of isometric actions on its compact, Euclidean, and noncompact factors. This fully reduces the classification problem for cohomogeneity-one actions to symmetric spaces of a single type.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示软材料大变形失稳与量子拓扑物理之间的深层联系，将两个看似无关的研究前沿——有限应变固体力学与量子拓扑物理——统一起来，为可编程智能软物质提供新理论路径。

Method: 将李群度量演化纳入广义Stroh形式体系，将高度非线性的几何受阻映射为代数表面阻抗矩阵H；对半无限超弹性半空间在有限压缩下，解析地将系统映射到一维狄拉克哈密顿量，其中宏观力学拉伸作为狄拉克质量的可调旋钮。

Result: 表面褶皱的萌生标志着从平庸到非平庸拓扑相的转变，表现为缠绕数的量子化阶跃，自然产生一个鲁棒的、宏观局域的零能边缘态。

Conclusion: 该基础性联系将宏观对称性破缺与拓扑范式统一起来，为可编程智能软物质开辟了新的理论途径。

Abstract: The macroscopic instability of soft materials undergoing extreme deformations is traditionally viewed as a pure structural or mechanical failure. Driven by the quest to uncover universal principles across disparate physical systems, we bridge two vibrant yet seemingly disconnected research frontiers: macroscopic finite-strain solid mechanics and quantum-like topological physics. Here, we demonstrate that the classical elastic surface instability of a deformed hyperelastic manifold is not merely a mechanical bifurcation, but fundamentally a topological phase transition. By incorporating Lie group metric evolution into a generalized Stroh formalism, we map the highly nonlinear geometric frustration onto an algebraic surface impedance matrix $\mathbf{H}$. For a semi-infinite hyperelastic half-space under finite compression, we analytically map the system to a one-dimensional Dirac Hamiltonian, where the macroscopic mechanical stretch acts as a tunable knob for the Dirac mass. We reveal that the onset of surface wrinkles marks a topological transition from a trivial to a non-trivial phase characterized by a quantized step in the winding number, naturally giving rise to a robust, macroscopically localized zero-energy edge state. This fundamental linkage unifies macroscopic symmetry breaking with the topological paradigm, opening a new theoretical pathway for programmable smart soft matter.

### [60] [Non-Perturbative Closure of the 3D $φ^4$ Field Theory via Operator-Valued Stroh Formalism and Barnett-Lothe Invariants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18635)
*Yu-Xin Xie*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个三维φ⁴标量场论在临界点附近的非微扰闭包框架，通过空间轴切片将 dressed 理论映射为无穷维辛李代数 𝔰𝔭(∞) 上的矩阵算子演化，推广了经典 Stroh 形式主义和 Barnett-Lothe 积分不变量。证明 dressed 算子值 Barnett-Lothe 张量满足恒等式 Ŝ²+ĤL̂ = -Î，结合 Källén-Lehmann 谱表示和 Schwinger-Dyson 方程，构建了"辛自举"主谱积分方程。该框架呈现精确维数约化，在2D退化为 Onsager 精确解 (η=1/4)，在4D退化为高斯平庸极限 (η=0)。求解强耦合共形不动点下的超越自举方程，得到非微扰异常维数 η≈0.0363，与最先进的共形自举数值极限吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绕过微扰费曼图展开长期以来在三维φ⁴标量场论临界行为中的局限性，建立一个严格的非微扰闭包框架，从而在不依赖微扰展开的情况下计算临界指数。

Method: 将3D欧氏空间沿空间轴切片，把 dressed 理论映射为 𝔰𝔭(∞) 上的矩阵算子演化；推广 Stroh 形式主义和 Barnett-Lothe 积分不变量到量子场希尔伯特空间；证明算子值 Barnett-Lothe 张量的代数恒等式；结合 Källén-Lehmann 谱表示和 Schwinger-Dyson 方程构建辛自举主谱积分方程。

Result: 得到了非微扰异常维数 η≈0.0363，与共形自举数值极限高度吻合；框架在2D精确还原 Onsager 解 (η=1/4)，在4D还原高斯平庸极限 (η=0)。

Conclusion: 辛自举框架为三维临界现象提供了严格非微扰解决方案，并揭示了与软物质后屈曲分岔之间的全息对偶性。

Abstract: We establish a rigorous non-perturbative closure framework for the three-dimensional (3D) $φ^4$ scalar field theory near criticality, bypassing the long-standing limitations of perturbative Feynman diagrammatic expansions. By slicing the 3D Euclidean space along a spatial axis, the exact dressed theory is mapped onto a matrix operator evolution governed by the infinite-dimensional symplectic Lie algebra $\mathfrak{sp}(\infty)$. We generalize the classical Stroh formalism and Barnett-Lothe integral invariants from anisotropic elasticity to the quantum field Hilbert space. Crucially, we prove that the dressed operator-valued Barnett-Lothe tensors satisfy the algebraic identity $\hat{\mathbf{S}}^2 + \hat{\mathbf{H}}\hat{\mathbf{L}} = -\hat{\mathbf{I}}$ exactly and non-perturbatively, regardless of the coupling strength. By coupling this symplectic invariance with the Källén-Lehmann spectral representation and the Schwinger-Dyson equations, a novel "Symplectic Bootstrap" master spectral integral equation is formulated. The framework exhibits exact dimensional reduction, naturally degenerating to the Onsager exact solution ($η= 1/4$) in 2D and the Gaussian triviality limit ($η= 0$) in 4D. Solving the transcendental bootstrap equation under the strong-coupling conformal fixed point yields the non-perturbative anomalous dimension $η\approx 0.0363$, matching the state-of-the-art conformal bootstrap numerical limits. Finally, a profound holographic duality between the statistical state equations and the post-buckling bifurcation of fluctuating soft matters is discussed.

</details>


### [61] [Self-averaging of replica overlaps in the random field Edwards-Anderson model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18752)
*C. Itoi,Y. Sakamoto*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了Edwards-Anderson模型中副本重叠的自平均性，并建立了EA序参量与自由能密度对随机场强度导数的关系，揭示了短程自旋玻璃模型与具有RSB相的均场自旋玻璃模型的行为差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Tasaki关联不等式，将副本重叠平方的期望值用EA序参量平方界定，并将EA序参量表示为自由能密度对随机场强度的导数（独立于边界条件），从而证明在无限体积极限下副本重叠的方差为零。

Result: 证明了在任意维度下，EA模型在耦合常数空间中几乎处处存在副本重叠的自平均性；同时也证明了无随机场的高斯交换相互作用EA模型中副本键重叠的自平均性。

Abstract: The self-averaging of the replica overlap is proven in the Edwards-Anderson (EA) model under random field almost everywhere in the coupling constant space in any dimension. The EA order parameter is represented in terms of the derivative of the free energy density with respect to the random field strength, regardless of boundary conditions. Tasaki's correlation inequality for finite-dimensional spin glass models shows that the expectation of the squared replica overlap is bounded by the squared EA order parameter. These simple evaluations enable us to prove that the variance of the replica overlap vanishes in the infinite-volume limit. The self-averaging of the replica bond overlap is proven also in the EA model with Gaussian exchange interaction without random field. Short-range spin glass models have been shown to behave differently from mean-field spin glass models with RSB phase.

### [62] [A finite element-based eigenvalue analysis for predicting thermal runaway in Li-ion battery packs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18983)
*Shailendra Rahi,Vinay Dhakal,Ankur Jain,Manish Agrawal*

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种基于有限元的框架，通过广义特征值问题的最小特征值符号直接判断热失控阈值，无需瞬态分析，在圆柱锂离子电池及电池组中验证了准确性，并系统分析了材料、边界条件、几何参数等对热稳定性的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热失控是电池系统及热活性设备中的关键安全问题，亟需可靠且高效的方法来预测热失控发生的条件，特别是针对几何复杂且传统解析方法难以处理的情形。

Method: 建立瞬态热传导（含温度相关内热源）的有限元框架；将问题转化为广义特征值问题，以最小特征值的符号作为热失控判据。

Result: 通过与圆柱锂离子电池及电池组的解析解对比，验证了方法准确性；系统分析了材料属性、边界条件、几何参数及空间变化热源对稳定性极限的影响。

Conclusion: 该方法无需昂贵瞬态分析即可直接预测几何复杂系统中的热失控阈值，为电池系统的热设计与安全评估提供了系统化、高效的工具。

Abstract: Thermal runaway remains a critical safety concern in battery systems and other thermally active devices, necessitating reliable methods for predicting the conditions under which thermal runaway may occur. In this work, we develop a finite element framework for assessing thermal stability in systems undergoing transient heat conduction with temperature-dependent internal heat generation. The formulation leads naturally to a generalized eigenvalue problem, wherein the sign of the smallest eigenvalue provides a direct criterion for determining the onset of thermal runaway. This approach enables direct prediction of thermal runaway thresholds in geometrically complicated problems without requiring computationally expensive transient analysis. The proposed methodology is validated through comparison with analytical solutions for a cylindrical Li-ion cell, as well as with a pack of cylindrical cells, demonstrating excellent agreement in both cases. Based on this model, the influence of material properties, boundary conditions, geometric parameters, and spatially varying heat generation on stability limits is examined. A key advantage of this formulation is its effectiveness even for complex geometries where analytical methods become impractical. By providing a systematic and computationally efficient means to identify stability thresholds, the present work offers a practical tool for the thermal design and safety assessment of battery systems.

</details>

### [64] [Bulk-boundary correspondence of (1+1)D symmetric gapped phases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19137)
*Yizhou Ma,Gen Yue,Tian Lan*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个算子代数框架，用于描述具有范畴对称性的一维能隙相的边界条件和体-边对应。通过构造半无限融合自旋链和交换投影边界哈密顿量，证明边界条件由模范畴的简单对象分类，并建立了体-边DHR范畴的对应关系，最终揭示体相系统是边界系统的丰富中心。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为具有范畴对称性的一维能隙相中的边界条件和体-边对应建立严格的算子代数框架，克服有限链近似方法的局限性，直接在热力学极限下处理问题。

Method: 从幺半融合范畴C、不可分解半单右C-模范畴M、指定体相的Q-系统Q∈C以及指定边界的右Q-模K∈M_Q出发，构造半无限融合自旋链和交换投影边界哈密顿量；利用DHR双模描述边界对称性拓扑场论；通过范畴论工具建立等价关系。

Result: 证明构造的哈密顿量具有唯一基态；实现了函子M_Q^op→BCond的等价性，即简单边界条件由M_Q的简单对象分类；边界DHR范畴与(C_M^∨)^rev幺半等价；体DHR范畴对边界的作用与Z_1(C^rev)的范畴作用一致；边界DHR范畴对边界条件的作用与(C_M^∨)^rev对M_Q^op的范畴作用一致。

Conclusion: 体-边对应被精确表述为：描述体相的丰富幺半范畴是描述边界的丰富范畴的丰富中心。这一结果将一维能隙相的分类推向更严格的数学基础。

Abstract: We develop an operator-algebraic framework for boundary conditions and bulk-boundary correspondence in one-dimensional gapped phases with categorical symmetry. Working directly in the thermodynamic limit, we construct half-infinite fusion spin chains and commuting-projector boundary Hamiltonians from a unitary fusion category $\mathcal{C}$, an indecomposable semisimple right $\mathcal{C}$-module category $\mathcal{M}$, a Q-system $Q\in\mathcal{C}$ specifying the bulk phase, and a right $Q$-module $K\in\mathcal{M}_{Q}$, regarded as an object of $\mathcal{M}_{Q}^{\mathrm{op}}$, specifying the boundary. We prove that these Hamiltonians have unique ground states and that the resulting realization functor $\mathcal{M}_{Q}^{\mathrm{op}}\to\mathrm{BCond}$ is an equivalence, so simple boundary conditions are classified by simple objects of $\mathcal{M}_{Q}$ and general boundary conditions by their finite direct sums. We also give a microscopic formulation of the boundary symmetry topological field theory using DHR bimodules of the boundary quasi-local algebra. For a half-infinite fusion spin chain, the boundary DHR category is monoidally equivalent to $(\mathcal{C}_{\mathcal{M}}^{\vee})^{\mathrm{rev}}$, and the canonical action of the bulk DHR category on it agrees with the categorical action of $Z_1(\mathcal{C}^{\mathrm{rev}})$. Finally, we identify the action of the boundary DHR category on boundary conditions with the categorical action of $(\mathcal{C}_{\mathcal{M}}^{\vee})^{\mathrm{rev}}$ on $\mathcal{M}_{Q}^{\mathrm{op}}$. This yields a one-dimensional bulk-boundary correspondence: the enriched monoidal category describing the bulk is the enriched center of the enriched category describing the boundary.

### [65] [Topology of Bloch Bands from Cauchy Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19141)
*Didier Felbacq,Emmanuel Rousseau*

Main category: math-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为先前工作中提出的反演对称一维周期介质的极-零拓扑形式提供几何解释，建立与Berry-Zak相位、实线丛等概念的几何联系。

Method: 利用反演对称性在柯西数据投影化空间上的作用，将极点和零点与Dirichlet和Neumann态（黎曼球面上Z₂作用的两个不动点）联系起来。通过布里渊圆通用覆盖上的Bloch特征向量构造，利用单值符号ρ描述实特征线丛的拓扑性质，并建立与之对应的局部系数系统。

Conclusion: 建立了极-零形式、Berry-Zak相位、实线丛和局部系数系统之间的统一几何框架。

Abstract: In a previous work, the topology of inversion-symmetric one-dimensional periodic media was characterized through the pole-zero pattern of an impedance-like function associated with Bloch waves. This construction reproduces the Berry--Zak invariant and provides a criterion for topological interface states.
  In the present work, we give a geometric interpretation of this formalism. We show that poles and zeros arise naturally from the action of inversion symmetry on the projectivized space of Cauchy data. The corresponding Dirichlet and Neumann states are identified with the two fixed points of the induced $\mathbb Z_2$ action on the Riemann sphere.
  The key observation is that Bloch eigenvectors are naturally constructed on the universal covering of the Brillouin circle. The topology of the associated Real eigenline bundle is encoded in the action of the deck transformation group on lifted eigenvectors. This action is described by a monodromy sign $ρ\in\{\pm1\}$, determined by the inversion representations carried by the band at the fixed points of the Brillouin zone.
  We show that this monodromy defines a natural rank-one local system over the Brillouin circle. The corresponding Real line bundle is classified by its first Stiefel--Whitney class, which coincides with the associated $\mathbb Z_2$ pole-zero invariant. This establishes a geometric connection between the pole-zero formalism, Berry--Zak phases, Real bundles and local coefficient systems.

### [66] [Ground state preparation of random all-to-all Hamiltonians using ADAPT-VQE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18339)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索是否存在量子算法能在模拟随机哈密顿量方面超越经典方法，特别是针对具有体积律纠缠的全连接随机哈密顿量（如SK模型和SYK模型）。

Method: 使用TETRIS-ADAPT-VQE算法，分别对稠密和稀疏的SYK模型（N=20马约拉纳费米子）以及量子SK模型（L=18个站点）进行基态制备，并评估其保真度、算子池大小和电路深度等效率指标。

Result: TETRIS-ADAPT-VQE能够以≥99.3%的保真度构建SYK模型（N=20）的基态，以≥99.9998%的保真度构建SK模型（L=18）的基态。SK模型的基态制备高效（算子池小、电路深度浅），而SYK模型（无论稠密还是中等稀疏）的制备效率不高。

Conclusion: TETRIS-ADAPT-VQE在SK模型上可实现高效且高保真的基态制备，但在SYK模型上虽能实现高保真度，却效率低下，表明不同随机哈密顿量模型对量子算法的适应性存在显著差异。

Abstract: The ground state of random Hamiltonians with all-to-all interactions such as the quantum Sherrington-Kirkpatrick (SK) model and the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model follow volume-law entanglement and are expected to be hard to model using tensor networks. In recent years, some progress has been made to push the limit of classical methods using neural quantum states. However, it remains an open question whether there exist quantum algorithms that could offer a quantum advantage over the state-of-the-art classical methods in simulating random Hamiltonians. In this work, we show that one such algorithm, TETRIS-ADAPT-VQE, can construct accurate ground states for dense and sparse SYK models containing up to $N=20$ Majorana fermions achieving fidelities $\geq 99.3\%$ and for the quantum SK model with up to $L=18$ sites achieving fidelities $\geq 99.9998\%$. We find that while the preparation of ground states is efficient (in terms of operator pool size and circuit depth) for the SK model, it is not efficient for either dense or moderately sparse SYK models.

</details>

Abstract: Out-of-time-ordered correlators (OTOCs) have emerged as a diagnostic of information scrambling and quantum chaos in many-body systems. We investigate the imprints of chaos in the dynamics of OTOCs in the Heisenberg spin-$1/2$ chain with random fields. The system is parameterized to exhibit a crossover from integrable to chaotic dynamics. We demonstrate numerically that the approach to saturation of the OTOC can distinguish between integrable and chaotic regimes, with a power-law $(1/t)$ relaxation for integrable systems and a higher-degree power-law decay $(1/t^α; α\ge 1)$ followed by an exponential relaxation for the chaotic regime. We also demonstrate that the relaxation and initial scrambling regimes exhibit distinct and universal features, with the former being sensitive and the latter being robust against different realizations of random-fields. ### [71] [Adiabatically-induced Kawaguchi geometry and jerk in quantum-classical systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16037)
*Athanasios Chatzistavrakidis,Larisa Jonke,Ryan Requist*

TL;DR: 本文通过近幺正变换对混合量子-经典系统进行绝热消除，推导出高阶有效作用量，发现三阶项导致非牛顿力学（依赖加加速度），并在经典变量空间诱导出具有近辛结构和含加速度微分线元的Kawaguchi几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在混合量子-经典系统中，绝热消除量子自由度会产生经典运动方程中的有效力。现有方法通常只考虑一阶效应，缺乏系统的高阶非绝热修正框架。本文旨在建立一套可推广至任意阶的绝热消除方法，以更准确地捕获分子动力学模拟中的高阶非绝热效应。

Method: 对量子态施加一系列近幺正变换，逐步消除量子自由度与经典变量之间的耦合，从而在任意绝热参数阶次上推导出经典变量的有效作用量。该方法系统性地生成了一个高阶力序列，其中三阶修正使运动方程依赖于位置的三阶时间导数（加加速度）。

Result: 三阶Euler-Lagrange方程呈现非牛顿形式，有效力依赖于加加速度。三阶项在经典变量空间上诱导出Kawaguchi几何，其结构由近辛结构和依赖于加速度（除速度外）的微分线元刻画。

Conclusion: 该高阶绝热消除框架能够高效捕捉分子动力学模拟中的非绝热效应，为混合量子-经典系统的多尺度建模提供了几何化的理论工具。

Abstract: Adiabatically eliminating the quantum degrees of freedom in a mixed quantum-classical system produces an effective force in the classical equation of motion. The elimination can be made to any order in the adiabatic parameter, generating a series of higher order forces. By applying a sequence of near-identity unitary transformations to the quantum state, we derive a hierarchy of increasingly accurate effective actions for the classical variables. The third order Euler-Lagrange equation is non-Newtonian as the force depends on the jerk, the third order time derivative of position. We find that the third order terms induce a special kind of Kawaguchi geometry on the space of classical variables. This geometry is characterized by an almost symplectic structure and a differential line element that depends on the acceleration in addition to the velocity. Our results can be used to efficiently capture higher order nonadiabatic effects in molecular dynamics simulations.

### [74] [Equilibration of generalized subsystems: a quantum-channel approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18360)
*Pedro S. Correia,Adalberto D. Varizi,Gabriel Dias Carvalho*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一的量子平衡理论框架，基于广义子系统的概念，将系统-环境结构和受限测量两种平衡情形纳入同一状态层面的描述。研究表明，当广义子系统的维度远小于被丢弃的微观信息的有效维度时，系统会达到平衡，且平衡态对初始微观细节不敏感。该框架还通过有限分辨率能量通道示例，揭示了残余有效相干性与谱多重性之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子平衡理论通常分别处理两种情形：一是系统-环境结构（复合系统幺正演化，子系统的约化态平衡），二是受限测量（粗粒化POVM或可观测量下的测量统计平衡）。缺乏一个统一的状态层面框架来同时涵盖这两种情况。

Method: 引入广义子系统的概念，将可访问的有效状态视为作用于微观状态的量子信道输出。推导了广义子系统平衡的界限条件，证明当广义子系统的维度远小于被丢弃微观信息的有效维度时平衡成立。进一步分析了典型初始状态在较大子空间中的行为，以及平衡描述对微观初始细节的鲁棒性。

Result: 建立了广义子系统平衡的界限条件，该条件在典型初始状态下可满足；证明了平衡描述对微观初始细节基本不敏感；该框架统一恢复了普通子系统和有限族POVM的平衡界限；通过有限分辨率能量通道示例，明确了残余有效相干性及其受谱多重性约束的机制。

Conclusion: 该工作为信息受限条件下的量子平衡问题提供了一个统一的状态层面理论框架，具有普适性，能够同时涵盖系统-环境结构和受限测量两种范式，并通过具体例子展示了框架的应用和物理内涵。

Abstract: Quantum systems governed by unitary and reversible microscopic dynamics may nevertheless exhibit equilibration, in the sense that some effective description becomes time-independent. Standard equilibration results usually consider two separate situations: system-environment structures, in which the composite system evolves unitarily while the system of interest equilibrates, and restricted measurements, such as coarse-grained POVMs and observables, in which the measurement statistics equilibrate. Here, we bring these descriptions into a common state-level framework using the concept of generalized subsystems, where the accessible effective state appears as the output of a quantum channel acting on the microscopic state. We derive bounds showing that generalized subsystems equilibrate when their dimension is small compared with the effective dimension of the discarded microscopic information. We further show that this condition is met for typical initial states in large subspaces and that the resulting equilibrium description is largely insensitive to microscopic initial details. The framework recovers the usual equilibration bounds for ordinary subsystems and finite families of POVMs. As an example, we also introduce a finite-resolution energy channel that maps unresolved microscopic energy levels into effective energy levels, thereby making residual effective coherences explicit and showing how spectral multiplicities constrain those coherences while strengthening equilibration. Our results provide a unified state-level formulation of quantum equilibration under general forms of limited accessible information.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前工作表明可从多熵度量（一类多体纠缠度量）中提取部分普适信息，但尚不清楚这些纠缠度量能在多大程度上从基态中提取普适信息。本文旨在填补这一空白，探索从基态纠缠中提取更丰富拓扑信息的可能性。

Method: 定义“局部非手性”流形的拓扑条件，证明在该条件下可从基态波函数的纠缠结构中提取拓扑配分函数Z(M)；通过分析四维流形的Pontryagin数，将局部非手性条件与四维T-SPT的存在性关联起来；设计相应的纠缠度量来检测这种非平凡T-SPT。

Result: 1) 证明了局部非手性流形可用于提取2+1d拓扑相中超越S和T矩阵的普适性质；2) 证明了四维中局部非手性流形的Pontryagin数为零；3) 建立了这一性质与四维超越上同调T-SPT的存在性之间的关系；4) 给出了一个能检测该非平凡T-SPT的纠缠度量。

Conclusion: 从基态波函数的体纠缠中可以提取比之前认为的更丰富的拓扑信息，局部非手性条件为分类可提取信息的流形提供了理论基础，且纠缠度量可作为探测超越上同调拓扑序的有效工具。

Abstract: We consider the problem of identifying a topological order based on bulk entanglement of the ground-state wavefunction. Previous work showed that some universal information can be extracted from multi-entropy measures, a class of multipartite entanglement measures obtained by applying permutation operators exchanging the degrees of freedom between different replicas of the wavefunction. It remains an open question to what extent such entanglement measures can be used to extract any universal information from the ground state. Here we show that the topological partition function $Z(M)$ of a manifold $M$ can be extracted provided that $M$ satisfies a topological condition which we term ``local achirality". We show that locally-achiral manifolds can be used to extract universal properties of 2+1d topological phases that go beyond the $S$ and $T$ matrices. As a first step towards classifying locally-achiral manifolds, we show that, in four dimensions, such manifolds have vanishing Pontryagin number. We relate this property to the existence of beyond-cohomology time-reversal symmetry protected topological order (T-SPT) in four dimensions. Finally, we present an entanglement measure that detects this nontrivial T-SPT.

</details>


### [76] [Characterization of nested Walsh parity-check filters in a single-photon eight-mode register on a cloud photonic processor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18408)
*Emma Tully,Jonathan Washburn,Megan Simons*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在Quandela的Belenos云端光子处理器上，利用单光子八模空间寄存器实现了两种嵌套的Walsh奇偶校验滤波器，分别对应经典[8,7,2]单奇偶校验码和[8,4,4]扩展汉明码。实验验证了泄漏抑制和综合征路由功能，在超过34万次探测中，中性输入直流端口泄漏平均0.6%，相比理想基线抑制约21倍；三个面奇偶综合征通道的选择性达94%-99%。文章还量化了校准偏移、编译散射等系统极限，并报告了一次Hong-Ou-Mandel退化事件。
